 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ALiqbP59">03.下载好的素材插入到Excel在中，先对小人ctrl+C，选中图表柱体直接ctrl+V，可得。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-6a97ca1fdc644477064ed48f51578682_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="481" data-rawheight="251" data-original-token="v2-6a97ca1fdc644477064ed48f51578682" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-bd5e0a0ed0ab700acf0eda686cd7ead1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="481" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-6a97ca1fdc644477064ed48f51578682_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   ps:这么丑的是正常的，千万别慌~
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Law04nf0">04.选中柱体单击2次，只选中一条柱体进行设置，我们再填充看到有三个选项，我们选择【层叠】即可。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-d92001300b546d6958646756cd9fc7ab_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="744" data-rawheight="595" data-original-token="v2-d92001300b546d6958646756cd9fc7ab" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-e9d024fe789c544cd3d520375d6d0459_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="744" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d92001300b546d6958646756cd9fc7ab_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3Zk2oAag">05.设置后可得到，比例正常的多人图形。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a9a64f5b2c4ebc0d1be1160a9c8b18f5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="374" data-rawheight="251" data-original-token="v2-a9a64f5b2c4ebc0d1be1160a9c8b18f5" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-9d082bc276ae9b5977ff6a7aa1ddbfde_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="374">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="SaGw0aPK">06.接着我们把另外一个女性图形，粘贴，用同样方法操作，可得到。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-18d18234d4f793c9786f72d5d42c1f98_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="480" data-rawheight="251" data-original-token="v2-18d18234d4f793c9786f72d5d42c1f98" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-40088c0201bf05bccd335ee7baee3ca4_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="480" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-18d18234d4f793c9786f72d5d42c1f98_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6RrjCAmc"><b>02【层叠并缩放】填充</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-957bc6469317dbd850a41d8bde306b22_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="535" data-rawheight="253" data-original-token="v2-957bc6469317dbd850a41d8bde306b22" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-453c89f4f8479a8e8a0e6c1bf7099c45_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="535" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-957bc6469317dbd850a41d8bde306b22_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="gdcJYAMC">01.上图中灰色部分是我们构造的辅助列数，选中数据，插入图表。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1978127e1756389e1edc16d04f333f79_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1052" data-rawheight="1002" data-original-token="v2-1978127e1756389e1edc16d04f333f79" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-9b4e50b06e1097b671fe3a9b05fc122a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1052" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-1978127e1756389e1edc16d04f333f79_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vijGsFnE">02.选中柱形图，记得点2次只选中一个柱体，分别复制2个灰色的小人进去。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-470f0b4a9619c239cb9f50aa1ee94c7b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="1255" data-original-token="v2-470f0b4a9619c239cb9f50aa1ee94c7b" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-2574091db9110aa5dcccb22a8f70fd4f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-470f0b4a9619c239cb9f50aa1ee94c7b_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>02.做一个总分的柱形图</h2>
 <p data-pid="TyUIP9S5">我们日常会经常遇到这样的【汇总统计表】，有每个月的业绩，还有每个人求和的小计。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-fa35e014c5dc7161f55cd28c90de51b1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="457" data-rawheight="185" data-original-token="v2-fa35e014c5dc7161f55cd28c90de51b1" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-5b2f9cd806a0baa51b2deaea9768434a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="457" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fa35e014c5dc7161f55cd28c90de51b1_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6X5qjYvf">有些同学经常做出这样的可视化效果，给这些数据都+上了数据条格式。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-05577079e8ef3ccd008ce373939a5f86_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="457" data-rawheight="155" data-original-token="v2-05577079e8ef3ccd008ce373939a5f86" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-a2a0a788eb95172c23c3d8a409706f4c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="457" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-05577079e8ef3ccd008ce373939a5f86_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="f7rmH_Z8">这样做的效果不是很好，可视化内容过多反而不能突出重点，下面用2招解决。<br></p>
 <h2><b>01条件格式+迷你图</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="OS1B57-x">条形图的条件格式能清晰看到各英雄间的对比，迷你图的趋势线能看到某个英雄各个月份之间的对比。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-8d339245c5029cb0af65d4d069ff0e4b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="521" data-rawheight="197" data-original-token="v2-8d339245c5029cb0af65d4d069ff0e4b" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-41e91e3278428d57218a42d63b8296a7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="521" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-8d339245c5029cb0af65d4d069ff0e4b_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nQ7KrE5s">01.选中汇总行内容，选择【条件格式】【数据条】，即可。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-d7dbe2cf8668486ba79020eb03b568ad_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="449" data-original-token="v2-d7dbe2cf8668486ba79020eb03b568ad" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-e460e65f6c4f9a559a9af1f95b7d88d7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-d7dbe2cf8668486ba79020eb03b568ad_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-e31c34c9d2379aeeb850976e0d2dec1a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="457" data-rawheight="155" data-original-token="v2-e31c34c9d2379aeeb850976e0d2dec1a" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-41da25a9c34b001b64e7b73d605115ad_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="457" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e31c34c9d2379aeeb850976e0d2dec1a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eNBUnqWh">02.在后面新增一列【趋势】，选择插入【迷你图】</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-fa62dcc94906d0f7d08e8ebaea58db0a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="521" data-rawheight="155" data-original-token="v2-fa62dcc94906d0f7d08e8ebaea58db0a" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-1ea27ead61588d0fbb9bba845e7f0200_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="521" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-fa62dcc94906d0f7d08e8ebaea58db0a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rKOH2jee">03.设置好数据源，以及迷你图要放置的单元格。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-c119b33104f98303551318872ed9f1c0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="884" data-rawheight="142" data-original-token="v2-c119b33104f98303551318872ed9f1c0" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="884" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-c119b33104f98303551318872ed9f1c0_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-71df4d63c0d8dfe9d4f15923c09f2a3f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="864" data-rawheight="280" data-original-token="v2-71df4d63c0d8dfe9d4f15923c09f2a3f" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1537813230f668a7c412d5ab7bf5adc2_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="864" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-71df4d63c0d8dfe9d4f15923c09f2a3f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wnTpanU_">04.双击向下填充。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-f9f39bb61b08731db436ade0b4d1dd42_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="600" data-rawheight="185" data-original-token="v2-f9f39bb61b08731db436ade0b4d1dd42" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a3560567eaa2b8e82a8db64ff7dbec89_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="600" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-f9f39bb61b08731db436ade0b4d1dd42_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="oDvtiVwa">05.把对应的高低点标记出来，数据显示更明显。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-bc090c1eefce17332d2271c7ba35b25a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="521" data-rawheight="342" data-original-token="v2-bc090c1eefce17332d2271c7ba35b25a" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-3b17a2c4345efa0030340049a65bead6_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="521" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-bc090c1eefce17332d2271c7ba35b25a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <h2><b>02总分柱形图</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="wQt1ylc0">技能清楚显示各英雄的比较，又能显示出每个月的细节。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-2dad5dbfed1c05e0243fbfd1a116bb4a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="640" data-rawheight="388" data-original-token="v2-2dad5dbfed1c05e0243fbfd1a116bb4a" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-09e5cbab8b1036ea1af040dfdeccc449_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="640" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-2dad5dbfed1c05e0243fbfd1a116bb4a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="JBor8zHa">01.选择数据源，插入柱形图。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-4af3909d3f774aca5d2892a8995fb190_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="905" data-rawheight="289" data-original-token="v2-4af3909d3f774aca5d2892a8995fb190" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-dca8e1d4f8ab3471455861a8fc2e9ac9_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="905" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-4af3909d3f774aca5d2892a8995fb190_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VZxxN94c">02.选中图表，切换行与列<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-13c4d2ad0419cd1e5054c31ca5ef236e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="598" data-rawheight="444" data-original-token="v2-13c4d2ad0419cd1e5054c31ca5ef236e" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-01fe4e43585c6f801f8daec7e4d047f7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="598" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-13c4d2ad0419cd1e5054c31ca5ef236e_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9VdQcO_d">03.右击【更改图表类型】，把【汇总】放置在次坐标轴上。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-f0b7a67f2cd7b6e7299613ac4cf25244_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="661" data-rawheight="529" data-original-token="v2-f0b7a67f2cd7b6e7299613ac4cf25244" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-e2c639698c5c43d5bbece3cca1d2af7d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="661" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-f0b7a67f2cd7b6e7299613ac4cf25244_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EhRr0I36">04.右击【设置数据系列】，把汇总的间隙宽度设置为20，包裹月份的柱形即可。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-5b973b73a9dd0f27010b1d9f81db64a1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="539" data-rawheight="343" data-original-token="v2-5b973b73a9dd0f27010b1d9f81db64a1" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-a5af6b188223fe9353dc729dcf520d98_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="539" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5b973b73a9dd0f27010b1d9f81db64a1_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-719e830171844c007efa72f0a655575a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="815" data-rawheight="390" data-original-token="v2-719e830171844c007efa72f0a655575a" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-54d76593e2d3653be56fecabd175dad5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="815" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-719e830171844c007efa72f0a655575a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="tjP9VYex">05.设置坐标轴最大值为450，保证汇总值一定高于每月的值。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-da28c4314f66be1ae89ca257c519bfb1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="822" data-rawheight="350" data-original-token="v2-da28c4314f66be1ae89ca257c519bfb1" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-46b9c1b16000b91c7f49e2675f9c14af_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="822" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-da28c4314f66be1ae89ca257c519bfb1_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PF2c2T56">06.右击【汇总】柱形，【填充】设置为渐变填充，保证看得到每个月的细节图。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-e108d0b6b32da21968de0ef3d52f8e81_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="495" data-rawheight="612" data-original-token="v2-e108d0b6b32da21968de0ef3d52f8e81" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-b37c9144daae67bb09fa3e3a5901d77f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="495" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e108d0b6b32da21968de0ef3d52f8e81_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="JmzRomhb">07.再+上标签和美化图表后，可得↓<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-105be18f9c057dcf045bd519a74e54de_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="640" data-rawheight="433" data-original-token="v2-105be18f9c057dcf045bd519a74e54de" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-bb29017ba60caf57e5b59e5ff26d958b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="640" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-105be18f9c057dcf045bd519a74e54de_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <hr>
 <h2>E05-2.进阶の条形图</h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-834c95995c40ee7eb27c16a501cbc5c3_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1394" data-rawheight="1374" data-original-token="v2-834c95995c40ee7eb27c16a501cbc5c3" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-7ef49eb0a788c8a8a586e0081f5f8508_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1394" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-834c95995c40ee7eb27c16a501cbc5c3_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 <h2>E05-4.进阶の组合图</h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-d8bb790920b413ca42012a73dc4f2114_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="560" data-rawheight="252" data-original-token="v2-d8bb790920b413ca42012a73dc4f2114" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="560" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-d8bb790920b413ca42012a73dc4f2114_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h3xsle5b">相信每个人都被各种考核指标折磨过，<b>销售额</b>与<b>目标完成率</b>就是魔鬼般的存在。这2个不同量级的指标放在一起，总感觉跟业绩一样别扭。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-0ab5fa797768fe82f69a55e09da0d98d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="260" data-rawheight="166" data-original-token="v2-0ab5fa797768fe82f69a55e09da0d98d" class="content_image" width="260">
 </figure>
 <h2><b>01组合图</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="agG4i8O4">①优点：作图简单。</p>
 <p data-pid="qjakhQe5">②缺点：2指标交织一起，要眼力好。</p>
 <p data-pid="H10QrA27">PS：这种作图时我们日常见得最多的作图方式。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-f1fefcf1c5717671351702495a265a9f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="675" data-rawheight="311" data-original-token="v2-f1fefcf1c5717671351702495a265a9f" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-86a7312cee1bda460900ae954514724e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="675" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-f1fefcf1c5717671351702495a265a9f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="42gS2jZM">01.直接选中数据源，插入组合图即可。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-6596a9fcbf2d435284dd0ca578e10d7f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="703" data-rawheight="550" data-original-token="v2-6596a9fcbf2d435284dd0ca578e10d7f" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-10d57bf0de637fc107b3e9d82fab0402_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="703" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6596a9fcbf2d435284dd0ca578e10d7f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="APxGweWF">02.这里选择推荐的图表，即可找到我们常规的组合图。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-bef3af313471688b0279c8c5ba04eaba_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="926" data-rawheight="434" data-original-token="v2-bef3af313471688b0279c8c5ba04eaba" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-f4159c147c5e90023562dd6da6f9cf5d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="926" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-bef3af313471688b0279c8c5ba04eaba_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1-GlRNo7">03.选择图表，利用【图表工具】→【设计】选项卡即可选中调整图表设计。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c26878f98b09b7eac4d35c362b4bb563_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="743" data-rawheight="551" data-original-token="v2-c26878f98b09b7eac4d35c362b4bb563" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-0ca93ce3b14964ca4b97f0291da69e18_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="743" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-c26878f98b09b7eac4d35c362b4bb563_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="c3faxbvU"><br><b>02还是组合图</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-07ca0b288f4af9074f28eae347283393_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="574" data-rawheight="330" data-original-token="v2-07ca0b288f4af9074f28eae347283393" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-71b9a2e122476ef18ce623773006946e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="574" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-07ca0b288f4af9074f28eae347283393_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="HMM3KQOf">难点：把上面的完成率弄成一样的长方形。主要利用了折线图的标记点填充为长方形，+数字标签即可做出这样效果。<br></p>
 <p data-pid="tSZKJG0B">01.插入组合图，选择更改图表类型，把完成率改为“<b>带标记的百分比堆积折线图</b>”，放在<b>次坐标轴</b>上。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-78c4597e2e25fa40b1cdc8c4af5ac3c7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="870" data-rawheight="599" data-original-token="v2-78c4597e2e25fa40b1cdc8c4af5ac3c7" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-b7b199436c5257525c9eef3081c49698_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="870" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-78c4597e2e25fa40b1cdc8c4af5ac3c7_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="tw3Q3sis">02.选中折线图，把线条颜色选择为无。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-2f2fee1633205559c904672d176734de_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="734" data-rawheight="288" data-original-token="v2-2f2fee1633205559c904672d176734de" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-aaa588e3c691c8ec9c49c9b1e270f3fa_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="734" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-2f2fee1633205559c904672d176734de_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4HSoyLkO">03.首先画一个形状，选中标记点后粘贴。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-802e745a98f44772ce126297919c28b5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="628" data-rawheight="318" data-original-token="v2-802e745a98f44772ce126297919c28b5" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-de1de993623d25f294fd5871dcf44f83_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="628" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-802e745a98f44772ce126297919c28b5_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="wtaP19hW">↓↓↓<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-07e840794a6eed33ac53afd12412ead0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="579" data-rawheight="334" data-original-token="v2-07e840794a6eed33ac53afd12412ead0" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1b89cc202596c51877813641ffb21dd6_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="579" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-07e840794a6eed33ac53afd12412ead0_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="QPT6V18x">04.经过一系列调整后，可得到效果如下<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-07ca0b288f4af9074f28eae347283393_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="574" data-rawheight="330" data-original-token="v2-07ca0b288f4af9074f28eae347283393" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-71b9a2e122476ef18ce623773006946e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="574" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-07ca0b288f4af9074f28eae347283393_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <h2><b>03堆积柱形图</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="oPpC4hut">①优点：作图难度★★</p>
 <p data-pid="TgSd6Mv0">②缺点：要自行处理数据源增加辅助列。</p>
 <p data-pid="3l2Fc2A6">PS：堆积柱形图的效果跟第02种效果相似，但作图方法不一样。难点在于增加作图辅助数据。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1ab694244c65c48ab3a0c1cce3818074_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="573" data-rawheight="327" data-original-token="v2-1ab694244c65c48ab3a0c1cce3818074" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-badf549e24d32da5da70a472f477cb42_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="573" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-1ab694244c65c48ab3a0c1cce3818074_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="NNHIXzG1">它是由堆积柱形图演变而来的，把中间填充为“无填充”，在上面的数据标签，引用为单元格的值。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-1eb00d55d4fbd89116ac7e5f9380b2ba_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="572" data-rawheight="327" data-original-token="v2-1eb00d55d4fbd89116ac7e5f9380b2ba" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-8def0fdb19e92c0bfe00bac7128605e6_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="572" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1eb00d55d4fbd89116ac7e5f9380b2ba_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="j2Y-_Mdo">01.改造作图数据，<b>销售额与完成率</b>为2列主要数据源，其他2列为辅助数据源。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-bc62f9c27a759da66de66949fd483a54_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="393" data-rawheight="334" data-original-token="v2-bc62f9c27a759da66de66949fd483a54" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-2fbbcd784fe93235642c0d6126769797_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="393">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ob-cYOdt">02.辅助标签每个数值都是相等，为保证柱形图的高度一样，且标签在上方。</p>
 <p data-pid="NPrsKHSU">每个柱子高度均：<b>月销售额X+辅助值Y +固定值</b>50</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-4f32be1b6de55de4cf1467b9705fa37e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="666" data-rawheight="327" data-original-token="v2-4f32be1b6de55de4cf1467b9705fa37e" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-6b9af67ebe91ddaf2b8e8953263752b5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="666" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-4f32be1b6de55de4cf1467b9705fa37e_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="yk0Bff6c">03.我们只需要用：销售额最大的值+设定的值-当月销售额，即可求出辅助列的值。<b>=MAXA($C$17:$C$24)+20-C17</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-7861618c158bdc5074a70dc493968ed7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="411" data-rawheight="358" data-original-token="v2-7861618c158bdc5074a70dc493968ed7" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-42998f660afdf964e4751c2ad5641f92_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="411">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="ePuE4uJ4">04.选择前4列数据，“完成率”那列不用选，插入柱形图。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-93ca79511db72deeec6bd7ccf057cf26_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="481" data-rawheight="289" data-original-token="v2-93ca79511db72deeec6bd7ccf057cf26" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c68cddedbdf5edbf3591b82306d6765a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="481" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-93ca79511db72deeec6bd7ccf057cf26_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="v5WWveoP">05.选中中间的，设置为无填充。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-ca74fb104d6cbe84dd89f828996d09fc_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="722" data-rawheight="300" data-original-token="v2-ca74fb104d6cbe84dd89f828996d09fc" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-9aa932a2f2d43a21c04b221cca456c55_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="722" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-ca74fb104d6cbe84dd89f828996d09fc_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="fnPqxOOO">06.选中最上的格，添加数据标签，右击设置，“单元格中的值”，点击选择范围。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-9a0cda244c01460436bd7b5c99ad61bc_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="867" data-rawheight="341" data-original-token="v2-9a0cda244c01460436bd7b5c99ad61bc" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-41370525884435f361b5b78c97d57386_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="867" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-9a0cda244c01460436bd7b5c99ad61bc_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y-HzClpe">07.选中完成率的标志，确定。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-a2c6b49c49ca0a22b993bdc3c7b1d498_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="673" data-rawheight="319" data-original-token="v2-a2c6b49c49ca0a22b993bdc3c7b1d498" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-87dd6621e710fc0eaf523bbab853416e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="673" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-a2c6b49c49ca0a22b993bdc3c7b1d498_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jdkrNL6o">08.再经过一系列美化后，可得：<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-31b18a2a85ef4542200e1f8dffb06841_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="578" data-rawheight="332" data-original-token="v2-31b18a2a85ef4542200e1f8dffb06841" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-fdee81828e16906ad69b791d97e1185e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="578" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-31b18a2a85ef4542200e1f8dffb06841_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <h2><b>04堆积条形图形图</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="w5WVh1ft">堆积条形图与上面的堆积柱形图作图原理是一样的。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-b4998aefba082a1426a5830f0189e8b7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="579" data-rawheight="317" data-original-token="v2-b4998aefba082a1426a5830f0189e8b7" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-91cd12cee9b5f2601b245ebb62e607eb_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="579" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-b4998aefba082a1426a5830f0189e8b7_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pCAtyimd">01.原来还是刚刚调整过的作图数据，把中间填充空白。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-95e4aee67be07ae9df1ebf1da58550d4_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="740" data-rawheight="272" data-original-token="v2-95e4aee67be07ae9df1ebf1da58550d4" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-11143d1479ab84c994bbb46fa7408bf2_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="740" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-95e4aee67be07ae9df1ebf1da58550d4_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <h2><b>05气泡图作图法1</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="7MHjkJ2J">①优点：显示直观，清晰明了。</p>
 <p data-pid="Iytt7dAb">②缺点：要大量处理数据，构造辅助列，作图难度：★★★★☆</p>
 <p data-pid="fTLXnlBL">③展示的效果，气泡大小表示完成率，柱形的高低表示销售额。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-bb1b9af93f25ea33055799399f225c9f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="572" data-rawheight="353" data-original-token="v2-bb1b9af93f25ea33055799399f225c9f" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-06318a4f80b801516043dce3557e2fc8_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="572" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-bb1b9af93f25ea33055799399f225c9f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="a5KZiqq6">01.首先，我们看看原始的数据源。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-795457a23c80cc48811b6ceacf3bab2a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="364" data-rawheight="325" data-original-token="v2-795457a23c80cc48811b6ceacf3bab2a" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-b0cc2fde9635b39c9e21b9491fced9aa_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="364">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DLzgFHx9">02.改造后的作图数据，需要增加了5列辅助作图数据，一共绘制3组合气泡图。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-5b34158490f25bbde3f53cecf3180538_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="643" data-rawheight="334" data-original-token="v2-5b34158490f25bbde3f53cecf3180538" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-13ded4ff4b29157ab1da388ac7959425_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="643" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-5b34158490f25bbde3f53cecf3180538_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="N2nNdrJm">03.根据数据源分别绘制了3组气泡图，依次用作展示完成率、销售额、月份。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-02698a9626930a9c7ace6f78b200ce3c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="640" data-rawheight="362" data-original-token="v2-02698a9626930a9c7ace6f78b200ce3c" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-a402052f1ebb55d49bae373ecb56b7f9_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="640" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-02698a9626930a9c7ace6f78b200ce3c_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LoMs5Oqf">04.把销售额和月份的气泡图，形状填充、形状轮廓均设置为无填充。<br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-02381504a2ef6fb6547cc1292c803673_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="876" data-rawheight="367" data-original-token="v2-02381504a2ef6fb6547cc1292c803673" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-d3171f9d479885412c8f6072bbf6ffa8_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="876" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-02381504a2ef6fb6547cc1292c803673_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="QE8ELZWG">05.设置误差线，勾选指定值，值的内容即为销售额。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-fd2320955dcdc4f735f8420703ba7e47_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="903" data-rawheight="488" data-original-token="v2-fd2320955dcdc4f735f8420703ba7e47" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c7afdbdb67be7f9767e91cd5e57aecfb_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="903" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-fd2320955dcdc4f735f8420703ba7e47_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="ZfUFYkBb">06.把选中误差线，把线条宽度设置为20磅。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-165269b9274edc0a23ed90d7551f22c5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="903" data-rawheight="488" data-original-token="v2-165269b9274edc0a23ed90d7551f22c5" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-9ee55ae9438d5a54b44d02b3cc02065b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="903" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-165269b9274edc0a23ed90d7551f22c5_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="GRJ3Da6C">07.更改线条颜色，和简单美化即可的。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-0dba1e6a473e49de86de61c7e9e0fadf_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="572" data-rawheight="353" data-original-token="v2-0dba1e6a473e49de86de61c7e9e0fadf" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-9f246a944ea03dddfa881508892e93ca_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="572" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-0dba1e6a473e49de86de61c7e9e0fadf_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <h2><b>06气泡图作图法2</b></h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-e31cbeacb984bef6285ee537f80c265b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="575" data-rawheight="396" data-original-token="v2-e31cbeacb984bef6285ee537f80c265b" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-22b46b792daaef0b03c78410b0719f6c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="575" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e31cbeacb984bef6285ee537f80c265b_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-294959b499ee61414cd6ebe27c74a942_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="643" data-rawheight="334" data-original-token="v2-294959b499ee61414cd6ebe27c74a942" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-b38d2f29978800bc85a1f28a6929d1e0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="643" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-294959b499ee61414cd6ebe27c74a942_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>

 <p data-pid="GQGvJikc">上面这些酷炫的动态图表，只是简单运用了<b>【Excel函数】</b>和<b>【切片器】+【透视表】</b>简单交互的原理。其实我们还有许多交互的方式，能做出动态图表。</p>
 <p data-pid="X5Xf9osb">做出酷炫的动态图表，最核心就是<b>【动态图表原理】+【合理布局】+【配色】+【合适的图表表达】=【酷炫的动态图表】</b></p>

 </figure>
 <p data-pid="_czmVjZO">今天主要跟大家分析【动态图表】，其他的已经分享过很多遍了，话不多说，上大纲↓</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-1f158eabdf2e009df47f64fb3354da00_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1398" data-rawheight="693" data-original-token="v2-1f158eabdf2e009df47f64fb3354da00" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1398" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-1f158eabdf2e009df47f64fb3354da00_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <h2><b>E00.动态图表原理</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="Kq71aZkE">因为Excel没有时间轴，无法描述运动轨迹，只能表达图表的最终形态。简单来说动态图表就是作图数据源发生了变化。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a5723086798244b536b4641945003255_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="603" data-rawheight="229" data-original-token="v2-a5723086798244b536b4641945003255" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="603" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-a5723086798244b536b4641945003255_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="Pf5_uK2Q">在Excel中常见的动态图表元素组合有：<b>选择器+抽数引擎+图表=动态图表</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-6b40ad234812f516f11d2935ba518480_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="757" data-rawheight="343" data-original-token="v2-6b40ad234812f516f11d2935ba518480" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="757" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-6b40ad234812f516f11d2935ba518480_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-fe576cfeb6c310f9e38f3dfba859cf29_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="963" data-rawheight="373" data-original-token="v2-fe576cfeb6c310f9e38f3dfba859cf29" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-3f0a4d04bbf471bbfdd8439ad54ad252_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="963" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-fe576cfeb6c310f9e38f3dfba859cf29_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   可以细分为以上组件要素
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6JS60SvJ">以下，我们根据选择器的不同，盘点各类动态图表：</p>
 <hr>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2><b>E01.</b>RANDBETWEEN<b>函数</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="Ih8OFHnl">我们可以看到构成RANDBETWEEN动态图表有三要素：<b>①数据源+②选择器→③动态图表</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-880aaae3cddabc0bdf03fa01a6224fcf_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-880aaae3cddabc0bdf03fa01a6224fcf" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-880aaae3cddabc0bdf03fa01a6224fcf_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

  </figcaption>

 <p data-pid="qAzMYHwe">04.个人作品示例</p>
 <p data-pid="qPqfHfXE">大家看到我大多数的动态图表，都是由randbetween函数构造的随机数值，通过刷新即可看到动态效果。</p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <hr>
 <h2><b>02.下拉序列</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="yz428JlR">下拉序列动态图表有4要素：<b>①数据源+②选择器+③作图数据源→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="ewgbsNJ8">控制链条是：②下拉序列<b>单元格→③作图数据源→④动态图表</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-45e56f8b42d2eeab03e21a0767e7c016_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-45e56f8b42d2eeab03e21a0767e7c016" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-45e56f8b42d2eeab03e21a0767e7c016_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   三级下拉菜单
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="uUcNDkqe">本道题目难点在于三级下拉菜单的设置，大多数人用到的是二级菜单做的索引，导致缺少了一级菜单的控制。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <hr>
 <h2>03.切片器+智能化表格</h2>
 <p data-pid="p94DbpeJ">智能化表格是普通小白最容易忽略，但在Excel中非常好用的功能。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-853a169a75374bbcc9ee963c1336857d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-853a169a75374bbcc9ee963c1336857d" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-853a169a75374bbcc9ee963c1336857d_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   课程案例：合同经营表
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-19cc22f86b935bddc0c769aee9c4d83f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-19cc22f86b935bddc0c769aee9c4d83f" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-19cc22f86b935bddc0c769aee9c4d83f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   仪表盘的制作↑
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="y5BRO8XB">Excel仪表盘其实可以拆分为：圆环图+饼状图，指针代表饼图，圆环图就是外边的颜色+数值</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <hr>
 <h2><b>04.透视表+切片器</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="GISvEVl0">切片器动态图表有4要素：<b>①数据源+②选择器+③作图数据源→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="JpWRvXO2">抽数引擎：<b>透视表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="v7UdLd4d">选择器：<b>②切片器</b></p>
 <p data-pid="kSqcH2s_">控制链条是：②<b>切片器→③透视表→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2><b>（1）一个切片器链接多个数据透视表</b></h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-96914e15a5342c7b1913a23635415c33_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-96914e15a5342c7b1913a23635415c33" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-96914e15a5342c7b1913a23635415c33_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JyMOZDGw">不少同学疑惑一个切片器控制这么多图表联动是怎样做的。其实原理很简单，就是切片器控制多个透视表。</p>
 <p data-pid="MzJfilqW">选择透视表右击，选择报表链接，把对应的透视表勾上即可。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-8f5b60732880228c26196da63ea7079f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="634" data-rawheight="353" data-original-token="v2-8f5b60732880228c26196da63ea7079f" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="634" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8f5b60732880228c26196da63ea7079f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>（2）多个切片器链接多个数据透视表</h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-777cac7e3ec55cbb055e273ba97d5c11_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-777cac7e3ec55cbb055e273ba97d5c11" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-777cac7e3ec55cbb055e273ba97d5c11_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="uThewjIJ">一个切片器可以控制多个数据透视表，当然一个透视表也能被 多个切片器控制的情况。这种情况下要注重我们的排版能力。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-291ab7da2f23d2f76af0ca712f10e70c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1362" data-rawheight="1416" data-original-token="v2-291ab7da2f23d2f76af0ca712f10e70c" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-8dbb130d46d5f6a085915e309ff70e66_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1362" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-291ab7da2f23d2f76af0ca712f10e70c_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>（3）一个切片器链接多个数据源</h2>
 <p data-pid="cgLdXN-q">不少同学很疑惑为什么切片器能控制多个数据源，主要我们把切片器选择的值链接到单元格上，然后用抽数引擎作为链接。</p>
 <p data-pid="BBxSgwJT">控制链条2条同时进行分别是：</p>
 <p data-pid="VqKM5dVH">链条1：②<b>切片器→③透视表→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="DA5LUxTp">链条2：②<b>切片器→③链接单元格→③作图数据源→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-40eb1abf4c774bd8a2087763fc25cb78_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-40eb1abf4c774bd8a2087763fc25cb78" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-40eb1abf4c774bd8a2087763fc25cb78_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   课程案例：科技风销售表
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-74ad14b4fc5eb3cc6dad9a0c119c8a9b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="806" data-rawheight="461" data-original-token="v2-74ad14b4fc5eb3cc6dad9a0c119c8a9b" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-0c0a90e474bd378b4b2fc1743d7fbaef_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="806" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-74ad14b4fc5eb3cc6dad9a0c119c8a9b_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   课程参考↑
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3oNyrRNb">​注：切片器无法直接链接多个数据源，可通过“<b>链接单元格</b>”间接链接多个数据源，要求有该数据源之间有“<b>相同的字段”</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Qsiz6wov">切片器动态图表有4要素：<b>①数据源+②选择器+③作图数据源→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="0mEsWRZE">切片器控制其他数据源要素：<b>①数据源+②选择器+链接单元格+抽数引擎+③作图数据源→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-6c276da41bdda92f37c17b1c913049c1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1081" data-rawheight="323" data-original-token="v2-6c276da41bdda92f37c17b1c913049c1" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c43e824ca7bfaa08e08665a201104ad9_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1081" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-6c276da41bdda92f37c17b1c913049c1_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q-INyzjZ">本案例中一共有2个数据源：<b>难点在于如何与第二个数据源的链接，只需要用一个链接单元格即可。</b><br></p>
 <h2><b>02链接实操</b></h2>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G35oQzEZ">01.首先我们要插入透视表后，接着插入切片器，利用2个数据源<b>共同字段</b>作为切片器筛选条件。题目中，2个数据源均有日期，于是利用日期作为切片器。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-db68d33fbf3146f63ea6d0d0b9b144ce_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="689" data-rawheight="185" data-original-token="v2-db68d33fbf3146f63ea6d0d0b9b144ce" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-2ac61055c01004a3c42dface7de4ea59_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="689" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-db68d33fbf3146f63ea6d0d0b9b144ce_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4A1ac_kI">02.我们把<b>切片器的字段移动到筛选区</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-b124490a9a0ac162f0f88b9ca040e46e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="645" data-rawheight="701" data-original-token="v2-b124490a9a0ac162f0f88b9ca040e46e" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-25f46bfe7dffee3d140616bc978cdf61_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="645" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b124490a9a0ac162f0f88b9ca040e46e_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ugxFFaiG">03.首先把切片器选择变化，从数据透视表直接用"="引用</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-8a78a3b56c8de77fb1c1d5a64a4d2583_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="929" data-rawheight="209" data-original-token="v2-8a78a3b56c8de77fb1c1d5a64a4d2583" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-56133d15b309568f00d5fdb091702b9c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="929" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8a78a3b56c8de77fb1c1d5a64a4d2583_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UOmUpUrv">=号引用的单元格充当了<b>链接单元格作用</b>。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="s9ij-Ubg">04.利用切片<b>器筛选的月份作为条件</b>，对<b>数据源2</b>进行统计汇总等，此处利用了<b>sumifs函数作为抽数引擎</b>。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-3b28e4d145ef1bcace342184d2bbcce5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="754" data-rawheight="119" data-original-token="v2-3b28e4d145ef1bcace342184d2bbcce5" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="754" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3b28e4d145ef1bcace342184d2bbcce5_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eiZQ2_ed">05.利用统计好的数据作为作图数据源，做出对应的 图表</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-e01b4aa1cfb7b065bad88a76b3e6331e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="808" data-rawheight="185" data-original-token="v2-e01b4aa1cfb7b065bad88a76b3e6331e" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-5638fd73a33ab24855c4c56b1b70d0d6_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="808" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-e01b4aa1cfb7b065bad88a76b3e6331e_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zUV2occq">06.当我们切片器选择变化的时候，链接单元格变化引起作图数据源变化，从而形成动态图表。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-40eb1abf4c774bd8a2087763fc25cb78_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-40eb1abf4c774bd8a2087763fc25cb78" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-40eb1abf4c774bd8a2087763fc25cb78_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>（4）切片器切换不同的图表类型</h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-753102dfc4b1f0297273094d43968015_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-753102dfc4b1f0297273094d43968015" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-753102dfc4b1f0297273094d43968015_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="B_jGMeDz">原理：<b>切换的图表不是真正的图表，而是链接图片</b>。本题主要利用了<b>定义名称，间接引用，链接图片</b>功能，如果看不懂做法，应该是对以上三个概念不熟悉。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8aYcEV97">​01.先根据透视表作为作图数据，做出各类型图表，每个图表<b>大小保持一致</b>。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-34456a5975abd915e9aff95713714e37_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="555" data-rawheight="148" data-original-token="v2-34456a5975abd915e9aff95713714e37" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-cad1278e16c653685ef3555707e1aa7b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="555" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-34456a5975abd915e9aff95713714e37_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ggI4Btox">02.依次对每个图表所占用的单元格区域，定义名称：<b>柱形图、饼状图、折线图</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-9e9e2a23c02eba556ae10273949688cd_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="624" data-rawheight="250" data-original-token="v2-9e9e2a23c02eba556ae10273949688cd" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-915b47da91647728932ca070390b56ea_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="624" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-9e9e2a23c02eba556ae10273949688cd_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-f7bedb349c23f22a4e3286c361c09e07_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="547" data-rawheight="86" data-original-token="v2-f7bedb349c23f22a4e3286c361c09e07" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="547" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-f7bedb349c23f22a4e3286c361c09e07_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="W4CO0zAQ">03.我要需要构建一个<b>新</b>的图表类型<b>数据源</b>，数据内容为我们刚刚定义的图表类型：<b>柱形图、饼状图、折线图</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5pjBRw9y">04.插入数据透视表，又在透视表插入切片器</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-583edb16f89cb071541d7315fac8e2be_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="461" data-rawheight="185" data-original-token="v2-583edb16f89cb071541d7315fac8e2be" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-b060a8043b772aca7cfaa67829d2f992_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="461" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-583edb16f89cb071541d7315fac8e2be_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EpxP5_FC">05.把图表的透视表，筛选出来的单元进行定义名称，我们此处定义为<b>“图表1”</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-181e98518b654f0374fc56ff42ad1a3e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="550" data-rawheight="237" data-original-token="v2-181e98518b654f0374fc56ff42ad1a3e" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-3b1ea51325d7419932c1593a45917bda_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="550" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-181e98518b654f0374fc56ff42ad1a3e_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ikx6hEZH">06.选择任意一个图表区域，复制，选择选择性粘贴，粘贴为<b>"链接图片"</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-0b7391fedda8b4f8b7e0f5c8d2c9ec2e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="537" data-rawheight="304" data-original-token="v2-0b7391fedda8b4f8b7e0f5c8d2c9ec2e" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c05c4e4c2607cb1e02bbb8cbfa9c594e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="537" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-0b7391fedda8b4f8b7e0f5c8d2c9ec2e_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2NVMd3FS">07.选择链接图片，在编辑栏输入<b>"=图表1"</b>，即可</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c956232cfa8eaa424763ab633e4efbfb_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="285" data-rawheight="291" data-original-token="v2-c956232cfa8eaa424763ab633e4efbfb" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-0651363615bdb69968ecd1d88a838455_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="content_image" width="285">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vfr6hA-N">05.关于数据透视表，还有更多经典的用法，如果对数据透视表不熟悉，日常又要分析大量数据的同学，建议学习一下数据透视表。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-2c9045aaf13f58cf2658bed753af8bc7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1280" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-2c9045aaf13f58cf2658bed753af8bc7" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1280" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-2c9045aaf13f58cf2658bed753af8bc7_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <ul>
  <li data-pid="aPI-Js2q"><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//study.163.com/course/courseMain.htm%3FcourseId%3D1209675830%26share%3D2%26shareId%3D480000002169511" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">点击学习Excel最强功能-数据透视表</a></li>
 </ul>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U3EvUDw2"><b>06.作品示例：</b></p>
 <p data-pid="IDcFnn69">透视表和切片器是最好的分析组合，我大多数<b>【数据看板】</b>作品都是利用透视表+切片器的。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-377cfaafd973c3221cf08f749b661473_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="560" data-rawheight="351" data-original-token="v2-377cfaafd973c3221cf08f749b661473" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="560" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-377cfaafd973c3221cf08f749b661473_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-49bb76c9d4fffaae19f132b6db4f339e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="560" data-rawheight="252" data-original-token="v2-49bb76c9d4fffaae19f132b6db4f339e" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="560" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-49bb76c9d4fffaae19f132b6db4f339e_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ufJh-xAQ">以上都是利用一个切片器联动多个数据透视表的效果，原理也很简单。选择切片器右击，<b>【报表链接】</b>，把对应关联的【数据透视表】前面□打√即可。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-8f5b60732880228c26196da63ea7079f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="634" data-rawheight="353" data-original-token="v2-8f5b60732880228c26196da63ea7079f" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="634" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-8f5b60732880228c26196da63ea7079f_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eUZO6PZg">在对应的透视表，插入透视图，当我们选择切片器时，即可得到这样的多个动态图表↓</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-fe1f13404e021a5e23d7e06beabf5c7a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="560" data-rawheight="285" data-original-token="v2-fe1f13404e021a5e23d7e06beabf5c7a" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="560" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-fe1f13404e021a5e23d7e06beabf5c7a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <hr>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2><b>E04.透视表+日程表</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="2bej5_ZZ">日程表动态图表有4要素：<b>①数据源+②选择器+③作图数据源→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="MKRYlxLR">抽数引擎：<b>透视表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="wiMg9aVq">选择器：<b>②日程表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="CrR8t1RR">控制链条：②<b>日程表→③透视表→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-e42f7eb58f5f49b9bfa6a98d390d5887_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-e42f7eb58f5f49b9bfa6a98d390d5887" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-e42f7eb58f5f49b9bfa6a98d390d5887_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   销售日程表
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="3vGFtzup"><a href="https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//study.163.com/course/introduction.htm%3Fshare%3D2%26shareId%3D480000002169511%26courseId%3D1210516801%26_trace_c_p_k2_%3D5bb4ce3c27ba41adb6d5511f84f36f64" class=" wrap external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer">1.点击这里获取以上Excel动态图表模板和练习</a></p>
 <hr>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="nVdgwrZ4"><b>二、Excel控件动态图表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="0_Dz4wkC">接下来的都是设计Excel控件的动态图表，Excel控件是在【开发工具】→【插入】。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-5cb3c9966ab49de28b05365b886d3392_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="475" data-rawheight="142" data-original-token="v2-5cb3c9966ab49de28b05365b886d3392" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="475" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-5cb3c9966ab49de28b05365b886d3392_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="Sb44KNQC">如果没有【开发工具】菜单，记得在【文件】→【选项】→【自定义菜单】，把【开发工具】勾上即可。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-677e97ff2cd48439d638411954422195_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="834" data-rawheight="647" data-original-token="v2-677e97ff2cd48439d638411954422195" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="834" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-677e97ff2cd48439d638411954422195_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p data-pid="k4RT6bws">因为Excel控件都是漂浮在单元格之上的控件，我们需要把控件的数值链接到单元格，所以这些控件都要设置链接单元格。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <hr>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2><b>E05.控件-组合框</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="luMf9JyL">控件-组合框动态图表有5要素：<b>①数据源+②选择器+②链接单元格+③作图数据源→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="R8zbET5F">控制关系链：②<b>下拉菜单→②链接单元格→③联动作图数据源=④动态图表</b></p>
 <blockquote data-pid="QjE3sjcj">
  与上面不同的是，控件的动态图表在②选择器上，多了一个链接单元格。链接单元格作用，链接控件与表格。
 </blockquote>
 <p data-pid="JIiRZObo"><b>（1）双指标的选择</b></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-a3dc5d523be5f461c6831dc5f2a8bbc1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-a3dc5d523be5f461c6831dc5f2a8bbc1" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-a3dc5d523be5f461c6831dc5f2a8bbc1_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>（2）综合对比选择</h2>

  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c218f6d9a5c0b1a02b34a8fab5d8a960_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="566" data-original-token="v2-c218f6d9a5c0b1a02b34a8fab5d8a960" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c218f6d9a5c0b1a02b34a8fab5d8a960_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <hr>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2><b>E06.复选框</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="mznyNN1C">控件-复选框动态图表有5要素：<b>①数据源+②多个选择器+②多个链接单元格+③作图数据源→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="516ST6u1">复选框：多个选框控制多个单元格。</p>
 <p data-pid="TgF0UuDz">制关系链：②<b>复选框→②链接单元格→③联动作图数据源=④动态图表</b></p>
 <h2><b>（1）显示不同类产品</b></h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-1f170a71f111f34c5bdffdd77e4ae4f2_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-1f170a71f111f34c5bdffdd77e4ae4f2" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-1f170a71f111f34c5bdffdd77e4ae4f2_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2><b>E07.单选框</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="aqnJvRAj">控件-单选框动态图表有5要素：<b>①数据源+②多个选择器+②1个链接单元格+③作图数据源→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="ubblgSzU">控制关系链：<b>下拉菜单→链接单元格→联动作图数据源=动态图表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="P8i4Hc7e">单选框：多个选框控制一个单元格。（注：一个工作表只能有一个链接单元格）</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>（1）实现自动升序降序</h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-f081446361438298b9a1cb49ff4db772_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-f081446361438298b9a1cb49ff4db772" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-f081446361438298b9a1cb49ff4db772_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 <h2><b>E08.调节数值器</b></h2>
 <p data-pid="RxfBkvZE">控件-数值调节器动态图表有5要素：<b>①数据源+②选择器+②链接单元格+③作图数据源→④动态图表</b></p>
 <p data-pid="498gUIO_">控制关系链：<b>数值调节器/滚动条→链接单元格→联动作图数据源=动态图表</b></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>E11.鼠标滑动动态图表</h2>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-28fa7916e089e0055fdcdb9fbb83a458_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-28fa7916e089e0055fdcdb9fbb83a458" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-28fa7916e089e0055fdcdb9fbb83a458_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   案例：鼠标点击滑动
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-ab0acff6e2e2ab9643d1fdb8d7b32733_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="622" data-rawheight="2119" data-original-token="v2-ab0acff6e2e2ab9643d1fdb8d7b32733" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-8761bfbac5f145d244d7e69818bd148b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="622" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ab0acff6e2e2ab9643d1fdb8d7b32733_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   图文教程
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <h2>总结：</h2>
 <p data-pid="hcDacd5a">在动态图表中，最完整可以拆分为：①数据源；②选择器；③链接单元格；④作图数据；⑤图表；⑥抽数引擎。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-57449e599ddc3bcdd8591b908c944e1a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-caption="" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="963" data-rawheight="373" data-original-token="v2-57449e599ddc3bcdd8591b908c944e1a" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-a24a52867ffce347b43d205c0805914d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="963" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-57449e599ddc3bcdd8591b908c944e1a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FCuksCLu">白色部分为具体的内容或例子的细分，细分部分具体要素，可以由另一个同类型要素代替。例如列表框可以代替列表框。</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a3dc5d523be5f461c6831dc5f2a8bbc1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="720" data-original-token="v2-a3dc5d523be5f461c6831dc5f2a8bbc1" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-a3dc5d523be5f461c6831dc5f2a8bbc1_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   这是组合框的样子
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-b3ebaa2fd06a1247db2be0e1955cfbb1_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-size="normal" data-rawwidth="1426" data-rawheight="753" data-original-token="v2-b3ebaa2fd06a1247db2be0e1955cfbb1" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-3d4aa451178d8ce4012050ab15f08df9_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1426" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-b3ebaa2fd06a1247db2be0e1955cfbb1_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
  <figcaption>
   这是列表框的样子
  </figcaption>
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Y_bwe8c5">当然可以互换不止选择器，抽数引擎、数据可视化表达形式，都是可以互换的，这就构造我们数据可视化的多样性。我们把系统的动态图表组合一起，就构成我们的【数据看板】</p>
 <p data-pid="HSvhOpCs">在每个图表的内容我们都有详细的<b>视频教</b>程和在课件留下了详细<b>的图文教程</b>，还搭配专门的<b>练习</b>，方便同学能进一步巩固知识点。由于篇幅的问题，就不一一把各项教程和课件罗列。有疑问和兴趣，可以在评论去留言呐。</p><a href="https://www.zhihu.com/zvideo/1239606815681933312" data-draft-node="block" data-draft-type="link-card"></a>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
